Insta Registration API

Patient Header Details

Get the minimum required patient data to be rendered on patient header

This endpoint returns the patient level information (i.e., mr_no, age, gender etc.,) to display in Patient Header. If request sent for advanced options, it returns visit information along with fields meta data.

REQUEST

GET

http://localhost:8080/instahms/patient/summaries/show.json{?mr_no,visit_id,appointment_id,advanced,header_preferences,visit_type,data_category}
Parameters
mr_no string

“MR00001” (Patient Unique registered MR NO. in the hospital)
advanced char

‘Y’ (default is ‘N’, ‘Y’ returns extra infor like visit etc., ‘N’ returns minimal set which is equivalent to the above api)
header_preferences

‘Y’ (default is ‘Y’, ‘N’ returns response without considering patient header preferences)
appointment_id String

10 (patient appointment without mrno)
visit_id string

This parameter will be ignored when
visit_type string

This parameter can have one of (‘b’, ‘i’, ‘o’) values. This can be sent multiple times. Default is array [‘b’, ‘i’, ‘o’].
data_category string

This paramter can be one of (‘Both’, ‘O’, ‘None’, ‘C’) values. This can be sent multiple times. Default is [‘Both’, ‘O’, ‘None’, ‘C’].

RESPONSE

Headers
Content-Type application/json
200 application/json
BODY SCHEMA 
                        {
  "appointment_details": {
    "patient_name": "INDENTA",
    "patient_contact": "999"
  },
  "patient_name": "INDENTA",
  "middle_name": null,
  "age_text": "26Y",
  "dateofbirth": null,
  "patient_gender_text": "Male",
  "patient_gender": "M",
  "expected_dob": "1990-12-29",
  "last_name": "",
  "salutation_id": "SALU0002",
  "salutation": "Mr.",
  "mr_no": "MR012835",
  "patient_contact": "999",
  "full_name": "Mr. INDENTA",
  "server_time": 1496652123912
}

REQUEST

GET

http://localhost:8080/instahms/patient/summaries/show.json{?mr_no,visit_id,appointment_id,advanced,header_preferences,visit_type,data_category}
Parameters
mr_no string

“MR00001” (Patient Unique registered MR NO. in the hospital)
advanced char

‘Y’ (default is ‘N’, ‘Y’ returns extra infor like visit etc., ‘N’ returns minimal set which is equivalent to the above api)
header_preferences

‘Y’ (default is ‘Y’, ‘N’ returns response without considering patient header preferences)
appointment_id String

10 (patient appointment without mrno)
visit_id string

This parameter will be ignored when
visit_type string

This parameter can have one of (‘b’, ‘i’, ‘o’) values. This can be sent multiple times. Default is array [‘b’, ‘i’, ‘o’].
data_category string

This paramter can be one of (‘Both’, ‘O’, ‘None’, ‘C’) values. This can be sent multiple times. Default is [‘Both’, ‘O’, ‘None’, ‘C’].

Update Patient Details From Header More Options

Update Patient Details

This endpoint is used to update the mobile and email id of a patient using more options.

REQUEST

POST

http://localhost:8080/instahms/patient/summaries/update.json
Headers
Content-Type application/x-www-form-urlencoded
application/x-www-form-urlencoded
BODY SCHEMA 
                          mr_no: MR00001
patient_phone: +918908907890
email_id: sunil.p@gmail.com

RESPONSE

Headers
Content-Type application/json
200 application/json
BODY SCHEMA 
                        {
  "mr_no": "MR0001",
  "patient_phone": "+918908907890",
  "email_id": "sunil.p@gmail.com"
}

REQUEST

POST

http://localhost:8080/instahms/patient/summaries/update.json
Headers
Content-Type application/x-www-form-urlencoded
application/x-www-form-urlencoded
BODY SCHEMA 
                          mr_no: MR00001
patient_phone: +918908907890
email_id: sunil.p@gmail.com

RESPONSE

Headers
Content-Type application/json
500 application/json
BODY SCHEMA 
                        {
    "error": {
                "status": 500,
                "displayMessage": "An internal server error occured"
             }
}
Get Patient Photo

Get Patient Photo

This endpoint is used to get patient photo.

REQUEST

GET

http://localhost:8080/instahms/patient/summaries/getPhoto.json{?mr_no,dimensions}
Parameters
mr_no string

“MR0001”
dimensions string

The valid values for dimensions are 36x36, 46x46, 66x66, 84x84. Id dimensions is not sent, the image with the original size will be sent.

RESPONSE

Headers
Content-Type image/jpeg
200 image/jpeg
BODY SCHEMA 
                        /9j/4AAQSkZJRgABAQEAYABgAAD/2wBDAAgGBgcGBQgHBwcJCQgKDBQNDAsLDBkSEw8UHRofHh0a
HBwgJC4nICIsIxwcKDcpLDAxNDQ0Hyc5PTgyPC4zNDL/2wBDAQkJCQwLDBgNDRgyIRwhMjIyMjIy
MjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjL/wAARCAABAAEDASIA
AhEBAxEB/8QAFQABAQAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAf/xAAUEAEAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA/8QAFAEB
AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAP/EABQRAQAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAD/2gAMAwEAAhEDEQA/AL+AD//Z
Upload Patient Photo

Upload Patient Photo

This endpoint is used to update patient photo.

REQUEST

POST

http://localhost:8080/instahms/patient/summaries/uploadPhoto.json
Headers
Content-Type multipart/form-data
multipart/form-data
BODY SCHEMA 
                          mr_no = "MR0001"
patient_photo = /9j/4AAQSkZJRgABAQEAYABgAAD/2wBDAAgGBgcGBQgHBwcJCQgKDBQNDAsLDBkSEw8UHRofHh0a
HBwgJC4nICIsIxwcKDcpLDAxNDQ0Hyc5PTgyPC4zNDL/2wBDAQkJCQwLDBgNDRgyIRwhMjIyMjIy
MjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjL/wAARCAABAAEDASIA
AhEBAxEB/8QAFQABAQAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAf/xAAUEAEAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA/8QAFAEB
AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAP/EABQRAQAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAD/2gAMAwEAAhEDEQA/AL+AD//Z

RESPONSE

Headers
Content-Type application/json
200 application/json
BODY SCHEMA 
                        {
    "status": "true"
}
Patient List Advanced Filter Options Data

Get All Filter Options Data

This endpoint is used for getting a master data for the filters provided in the Advanced Search Screen.

GET

http://localhost:8080/instahms/patients/getFilterData.json{?flow_id}

flow_id string

“OP Flow” (flow name)

Patient List Saved Searches List

List all saved searches

This endpoint is used for getting a list of all patient list saved searches.

REQUEST

GET

http://localhost:8080/instahms/savedsearches/getSearches.json{?flow_id}
Parameters
flow_id string

OP Flow (flow name)

RESPONSE

Content-Type application/json
200 application/json

Patients List

List all patients

This endpoint is used for getting a list of all patients

REQUEST

GET

http://localhost:8080/instahms/patients/list.json{?status,page_num,page_size,sort_order,sort_reverse,search_id,appointment_date,visit_date,visit_status,bill_status,patient_status,doctor,department,_department_type,primary_insurance,secondary_insurance,find_string}
Parameters
status char

‘A’ (A for active,I for inactive)
page_num int

1 (which page number to fetch?)
page_size int

20 (number of items in a page)
sort_order string

“region name” (name of the field on which to sort)
sort_reverse boolean

true (sort in ascending or descending; will only work if sortOrder is specified)
search_id int

10 (id of the search name, when present ignore query params get the patient list based on this parameter)
appointment_date string[]

“15-03-2017” (get all the appointments from this date)
visit_date string[]

“15-03-2017” (get all the visits starting this date)
visit_status char[]

‘A’ (A for active, I for inactive and N for No visits, “ indicates All)
bill_status char[]

‘O’ (O for Open, F for finalized, C for Closed, X for Cancelled)
patient_status string[]

“Consultation Pending”
doctor string[]

“DOC001”, “DOC002”
department string[]

“DEP0001”, “DEP0002”
_department_type string

“consultation”
primary_insurance string[]

“ICM00001”, “ICM00002”
secondary_insurance string[]

“ICM00001”, “ICM00002”
find_string string

“Kamal” (search by mrno or patientname or governement identifier or patient phone)

RESPONSE

Headers
Content-Type application/json
200 application/json
BODY SCHEMA

List all patients (Advanced search)

This endpoint is used for getting a list of all patients

REQUEST

GET

http://localhost:8080/instahms/patients/advanceList.json{?status,page_num,page_size,sort_order,sort_reverse,search_id,appointment_date,visit_date,visit_status,bill_status,patient_status,doctor,department,_department_type,primary_insurance,secondary_insurance,find_string}
Parameters
status char

‘A’ (A for active,I for inactive)
page_num int

1 (which page number to fetch?)
page_size int

20 (number of items in a page)
sort_order string

“region name” (name of the field on which to sort)
sort_reverse boolean

true (sort in ascending or descending; will only work if sortOrder is specified)
search_id int

10 (id of the search name, when present ignore query params get the patient list based on this parameter)
appointment_date string[]

“15-03-2017” (get all the appointments from this date)
visit_date string[]

“15-03-2017” (get all the visits starting this date)
visit_status char[]

‘A’ (A for active, I for inactive and N for No visits, “ indicates All)
bill_status char[]

‘O’ (O for Open, F for finalized, C for Closed, X for Cancelled)
patient_status string[]

“Consultation Pending”
doctor string[]

“DOC001”, “DOC002”
department string[]

“DEP0001”, “DEP0002”
_department_type string

“consultation”
primary_insurance string[]

“ICM00001”, “ICM00002”
secondary_insurance string[]

“ICM00001”, “ICM00002”
find_string string

“Kamal” (search by mrno or patientname or governement identifier or patient phone)

RESPONSE

Headers
Content-Type application/json
200 application/json
BODY SCHEMA 
                        {

Lookup Registered Patients

Search for registered patients

REQUEST

GET

http://localhost:8080/instahms/patients/lookup.json{?q,search_on,match_type,page_num,page_size,filters}
Parameters
q string

Search for a string
search_on enum mr_no

Limit search scope to a field. If not provided searches on all fields. valid values : mr_no, name, phone_number, government_identifier
match_type enum ends_with

Select matching strategy. If not provided uses ends_with for mr_no and government_identifier, starts_with for phone_number and contains for name. Valid Values : ends_with, starts_with, contains, exact_match
page_num number

select page number for paginated result set.
page_size number

select results to return per size for paginated result set. Valid values between 1 and 100.
filters enum skip_duplicate_mrno

Apply predefined data filters . skip_duplicate_mrno removes all patients marked as duplicate from result set.

RESPONSE

Headers
Content-Type application/json
200 application/json
BODY SCHEMA 
                        {
    page_size: 15,
    patients: [
        {
            oldmrno: null,
            patient_name: "Panini",
            government_identifier: null,
            middle_name: "Brijesh",
            age_text: "50Y",
            patient_phone_country_code: "+91",
            patient_gender: "M",
            dob: "24-09-1966",
            last_name: "Shukla",
            patient_phone: "+919853574728",
            mr_no: "MR001234",
            full_name: "Panini Brijesh Shukla"
        }
    ],
    page_num: 1,
    total_records: 1
}
